The notes for each voice are hold in a track and you can assign an arbitrary sound to each track to give it its specific character. So you can arrange the song in a creative way and create and publish your own interpretations.\r\nMany of the midi files are free (for example: Mutopia Project with tousends of songs), others are copyright protected and have to be purchased.\r\nThe SoundDesigner Music Creator contains a collection of 4 synthesizer engines: GM Bank, Additive Synthesizer, Waveform Modulator and Sampler.
